< Review>
Bathrooms are usually dirty,,and out of supplies, the reason it's usually easy to find a parking place is because most people that live in the area know" not go to the Park alone especially after dark.
I think a wise person would apply these cautionary statements to 75% of the parks in our country, it's just the day in age we live in.
Fontana PD patrols regularly.
Numerous large trees provide lots of shade.
Grass, shrubs and trees are all well maintained.
The large, elaborate play areas for the young people in our lives ( I would guess) are always popular.
I would have given a higher rating for more dog waste cleanup, watering stations for our furry<//Review>

< text>
The atmosphere at the Whitebark Restaurant & Lounge is very cozy. The fireplace, the open bar, and window seating. The food was tasty and the coffee was fresh and strong. A bit pricey but you are paying to eat at a hotel restaurant and the ambiance. The downfall is the extremely poor service. We waited to be approach to be seated until a line of customers formed and the woman behind us had to flag someone down. Once seated it took awhile for the server to come with menus. The food took a long time to come to the table and forget getting a second cup of coffee. We literally had to ask servers as they walked by our table. One server, in particular, had to have heard us but intentionally walked by. The couple who sat at the same time we did, had the manager come over so she could formally complain at how long it took to get her order and it was wrong. Could have been a poor crew this one day, I'll offer that. But my review stays at a very low 3.</text>

< review>
Tried this place for something different. With the price and location, I expected much more. I walked in to pick up a to-go order and no one greeted me. After a few minutes, I walked up to the bar. No one said a word. I then grabbed a server and asked how to pick up food and he hastily pointed saying "in the back." Umm... Back where? Definitely lacking customer service.

The food. We ordered a quesadilla, lobster mac and cheese and crab cakes. I saw the price and figured they must be good. The quesadilla was okay. Not quite enough cheese for the tortilla. I expected a whole quesadilla, not a half. The lobster mac was like eating Kraft boxed white cheddar mac and cheese. No cheesiness to it. No flavor. Nothing. There were also lobster shells. Overall, Knoll's was okay. I doubt I would return. If I did, it would not be anytime soon. Photos have been posted.<//review>

One side is the restaurant side, if you want more of a quiet and romantic dinning experience. The other side is the bar. The actual bar shape is a u . The bar is beautiful. The food is fantastic, our favorite is Signature pizza and the Boom boom shrimp. Let's not forget the Korean steak Taco's yummmmmmy. üòÄ If you love to be entertained by an accomplished guitarist, songwriter/composer and vocalist then Mike Hamilton is a must see. Mike has recorded with several artists Stevie Nick's, Sting, Bette Midler just to name a few. You can catch him on Saturday nights playing at the Knolls.</text>

I went there to buy myself skis and ski boots. Staff was personable and friendly. 21st anniversary prices were pretty good. Had to become a member in order to benefit. My skis weren't available in the right size. Had to be ordered and transferred from another store. I paid for everything (including work on the bindings) and waited for the store to notify me. This is when the minor confusion started. When I was notified, the staff hadn't worked on the bindings, despite their internal memo. It turned out that the skis were at the front office but needed to be transferred to the back office. At first, it looked like I had to come back a couple of days later. However, one of the staff members remembered me and was able to work on the bindings right away. 15 minutes later I was done and happy. Overall, good experience. <name>Jeffrey Purganan< /name><Time>1542261436159</Time><rate>5< /rate>< Review>
With so many stores closing it is refreshing to visit a store with an emphasis on community and customer service! I have also participated in some of the running groups that meet at the store and hope to connect with other community groups as my kids are beginning to ski and hike.

As a brick and mortar store, there is lots of great gear and a healthy rotation of seasonal clothing. I am always happy with the in store selection... even if I don't buy something, I leave with a better idea of what I really need/want. So, while very few of us get everything in one place when it comes to sports and outdoor equipment, Sports Basement is always a stop on my search.

Finally, they have competitive prices, discounts for members (on top of their typically lower prices), used and last season gear sales, and support a local charity of choice should you choose to designate one.</Review>

I came here for the first time today, and I am already in love.  Sports stores are already dangerous territory for me since I love buying running accessories, and sports basement has an incredible selection at even better prices.  When I took a look at their shoe selection for example, I noticed that shoes were between $10 - $20 cheaper than I have been able to find anywhere else.

They literally have everything you could possibly ever want for your athletic needs.  The even better part is that their staff is super friendly and knowledgeable.  Each person is very involved in at least one sport, so it was easy to ask opinions about the merchandise. I also started reading other people's reviews just now and realized that they have free classes (yoga, pilates, core) and a running club.  This place is honestly a dream come true for a fitness junkie like me.  I'm so happy that I came across it and I will absolutely be back again soon to try some of their classes and go on yet another fitness shopping spree!</text>
